## what's up?; what's wrong?
### zÄ›nme le
---
- **definition:** what's up?; what's wrong?
- **pinyin:** zÄ›nme le
- **components:**

- **etymology:**

  - **description:** æ€ä¹ˆ (zÄ›nme, how/why) + äº† (le, sentence-final particle indicating a new situation) = inquiry about what happened/what's wrong.

### çˆ¸çˆ¸(çˆ¸çˆ¸) â†’ çˆ¸(çˆ¸) â†’ å·´(å·´)
- **definition:** to long for; to cling
- **pinyin:** bÄ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Pictogram â€” a huge snake; however, in é‚‘ and è‰² it represents a person kneeling.
  - **interpretation:** Originally depicted a large snake with a curved body, giving it a simple, iconic shape. ## alright; fine
